# ::id dip_test_0001.1
# ::snt ITALY message AUSTRIA that Hey Austria! I know AT is one of the least successful alliances in the game, so I'm super down to work together here, especially if we can get Russia and Turkey fighting.
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Italy"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Austria"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c2
                        :op2 c)
                  :ARG3 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Italy")))
            :ARG2 c2)
      :ARG3 c3)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 AUS :ARG1 ALY (AUS ITA) VSS (ITA) :ARG2 AUS))

# ::id dip_test_0001.2
# ::snt FRANCE message GERMANY that Hey Germany! Just reaching out to say I think our two nations tend to benefit a ton from working together, and I'm very down to work together if you'd be interested!
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany"))))
            :ARG2 c2)
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 ALY (FRA GER) :ARG2 ENG))

# ::id dip_test_0001.3
# ::snt FRANCE message ITALY that Hey Italy! I think our two nations tend to do best when we can leave each other alone, so I'd love it if we could agree to not harass one another?
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (a / attack-01
                  :polarity -
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Italy")))
            :ARG2 c3)
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 (attack-01 :polarity "-" :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 ITA) :ARG2 ITA))

# ::id dip_test_0001.5
# ::snt TURKEY message RUSSIA that Hey Russia, just wanna say good luck and hopefully we can be friends!
AMR:
(t / tell-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Italy"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Russia"))))
            :ARG3 c)
      :ARG2 c3)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: (tell-01 :ARG0 AUS :ARG1 PRP (ALY (AUS RUS)) :ARG2 RUS)

# ::id dip_test_0001.6
# ::snt AUSTRIA message ITALY that I'm also down! Have you heard from either of them yet?
AMR:
(t / tell-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG1 (s / support-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (m / move-01
                  :ARG1 (u / unit
                        :mod (c2 / country
                              :name (n2 / name
                                    :op1 "Italy")))
                  :ARG2 (p / province
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Tunisia"))))
      :ARG2 (c3 / country
            :name (n4 / name
                  :op1 "Germany")))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: (tell-01 :ARG0 AUS :ARG1 AUS SUP (unit :mod ITA) MTO TUN :ARG2 GER)

# ::id dip_test_0001.7
# ::snt ENGLAND message FRANCE that Hey France! I think we both have bigger concerns than each other so I'd like to propose an alliance between us. Would you be willing to agree to a DMZ in the Channel?
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "England"))
      :ARG1 (p2 / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Germany"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c2
                        :op2 c))
            :ARG3 (c3 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "France")))
      :ARG3 c2)
PARA-DAIDE: PRP (PRP (ALY (GER ENG)))

# ::id dip_test_0001.12
# ::snt FRANCE message ENGLAND that Hey England! I'm more than happy to agree to that, I think our nations tend to do best when we don't harass one another. Would you like to focus together on attacking Germany, or would you rather move in separate directions?
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "France"))
            :ARG1 (a2 / agree-01
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (a3 / attack-01
                        :ARG0 (a4 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "England")))
                        :ARG1 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany")))
                  :ARG2 c2)
            :ARG2 c3)
      :op2 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 c3
            :ARG1 (a5 / attack-01
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 (c4 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Germany")))
            :ARG3 c)
      :ARG3 c4)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (tell-01 :ARG0 FRA :ARG1 YES (attack-01 :ARG0 AND FRA ENG :ARG1 GER) :ARG2 GER) (PRP (attack-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 GER))

# ::id dip_test_0001.13

                        :op1 "Germany"))
            :ARG1 (c3 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Italy"))
            :ARG2 c)
      :ARG2 c3)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: (tell-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 (tell-01 :ARG0 GER :ARG1 ITA :ARG2 ENG) :ARG2 ITA)

# ::id dip_test_0001.18
# ::snt ITALY message RUSSIA that Hey Russia! I love an R/I, and I think it's one of the more effective alliances in the game. What do you say we work together to take out Turkey and then Austria?

      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name

                  :op1 c

                  :op3 (c3 / country

      :ARG3 c2)
DAIDE: PRP (ALY (ITA RUS AUS) VSS (TUR))

# ::id dip_test_0001.19
# ::snt ENGLAND message RUSSIA that Hey Russia! I'd like to take Norway this year, but I'm not planning on sending any further units your way. If there's anything I can do to help you, feel free to ask!
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (t / tell-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Russia"))
                  :ARG1 (h / have-03
                        :ARG0 c
                        :ARG1 (p2 / province
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Norway"))
                        :time (d / date-entity
                              :year 1902))
                  :ARG2 (c3 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Russia")))
            :ARG3 c2)
      :op2 (p3 / propose-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (t2 / tell-01
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 h
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 p2
                  :time d
                  :year 1902)
            :ARG2 c3)
      :ARG3 c3)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 SCD (ENG NWY) :ARG2 RUS))) (PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 SCD (ENG NWY) :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 NWY :time (date-entity :year "1902") :year "1902")))

# ::id dip_test_0001.26
# ::snt FRANCE message ITALY that Excellent! I feel the same way, so I look forward to our alliance! Would you be alright with a DMZ in Pie, Gol, and W Med?
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "France"))
            :ARG1 (a2 / ally-01
                  :ARG1 c
                  :ARG2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Italy")))
            :ARG2 c2)
      :op2 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (a3 / and
                  :op1 (d / demilitarize-01
                        :ARG1 (a4 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 c2)
                        :ARG2 (a5 / and
                              :op1 (p2 / province
                                    :name (n3 / name
                                          :op1 "Piedmont"))
                              :op2 (p3 / province
                                    :name (n4 / name
                                          :op1 "Greece"))
                              :op3 (p4 / province
                                    :name (n5 / name
                                          :op1 "Greece"))))
                  :op2 d
                  :ARG1 (a6 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG2 (a7 / and
                        :op1 (p5 / province
                              :name (n6 / name
                                    :op1 "Piedmont"))
                        :op2 (p6 / province
                              :name (n7 / name
                                    :op1 "Wales")))))
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (tell-01 :ARG0 FRA :ARG1 ALY (FRA) :ARG2 ITA) (PRP (AND (DMZ (FRA ITA) (PIE GRE GRE)) (DMZ (FRA ITA) (PIE GRE GRE))))

# ::id dip_test_0001.27

                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "London")))
                  :ARG3 (c3 / country)
                  :ARG3 c2)
            :ARG3 c2))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 PRP (XDO ((fleet :mod ENG) CVY AMY CTO LON)) :ARG3 ENG))

# ::id dip_test_0001.31
# ::snt ENGLAND message RUSSIA that I don't think I can do that; it would leave me completely open to France. However, I am planning on taking it with a fleet.
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (p / possible-01
                  :polarity -
                  :ARG1 (h / have-03
                        :ARG0 c
                        :ARG1 (p2 / province
                              :name (n2 / name
                                    :op1 "Marseille"))))
            :ARG2 (c2 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Russia")))
      :op2 t
      :ARG0 c
      :ARG1 (p3 / possible-01
            :ARG1 (h2 / have-03
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (p4 / province
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Burgundy"))))
      :ARG2 c2
      :op3 (e / expect-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (h3 / have-03
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 p4)))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (tell-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 (possible-01 :polarity "-" :ARG1 (have-03 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 MAR)) :ARG2 RUS) (tell-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 (possible-01 :polarity "-" :ARG1 (have-03 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 MAR)) :ARG2 RUS) (expect-01 :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 (have-03 :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 BUR))

# ::id dip_test_0001.32
# ::snt RUSSIA message AUSTRIA that Hey Austria, sounds good to me! Bounce Galicia and work together sounds good to me, I think the R/A is one of the more powerful alliances on the board.
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Russia"))
            :ARG1 (p / propose-01
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (b / bounce-03
                        :ARG1 (u / unit
                              :mod c)
                        :ARG2 (u2 / unit
                              :mod (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "Austria")))
                        :ARG3 (p2 / province
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Galicia")))
                  :ARG3 c2)
            :ARG2 c2)
      :op2 (a2 / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a3 / and
                  :op1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Italy"))
                  :op2 c)))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (tell-01 :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 PRP ((bounce-03 :ARG1 (unit :mod RUS) :ARG2 (unit :mod AUS) :ARG3 GAL)) :ARG2 AUS) (ALY (ITA RUS))

# ::id dip_test_0001.35
# ::snt ENGLAND message AUSTRIA that I have. He wants me to not take Norway with an army. Which is fine by me but I'm not going to oblige. What do you think of him?

      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country

            :ARG2 c2)

            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 p
            :ARG3 c2))

# ::id dip_test_0001.513
# ::snt FRANCE message GERMANY that Personally I'd prefer that you wait till the fall to take it, that way I can move to Burgundy in the Spring to set up an attack on Belgium in the fall and not have to worry about the army in Belgium retreating into Burgundy and threatening Marseilles. Would you be okay with waiting until the fall to take Belgium?
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "France"))
            :ARG1 (p / propose-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Germany"))
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 (a3 / attack-01
                              :ARG0 c
                              :ARG1 (p2 / province
                                    :name (n3 / name
                                          :op1 "Belgium")))
                        :op2 (m / move-01
                              :ARG1 (u / unit
                                    :mod c)
                              :ARG2 (p3 / province
                                    :name (n4 / name
                                          :op1 "Burgundy"))
                              :time (d / date-entity
                                    :year 1904
                                    :season (f / fall)))
                        :op3 (a4 / attack-01
                              :ARG0 (a5 / and
                                    :op1 c
                                    :op2 c2)
                              :ARG1 (p4 / province
                                    :name (n5 / name
                                          :op1 "Belgium"))
                              :time (d2 / date-entity
                                    :year 1904
                                    :season (s / spring))))
                  :ARG3 c)
            :op2 (p5 / propose-01
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (a6 / and
                        :op1 (r / retreat-01
                              :ARG1 (a7 / army
                                    :mod (c3 / country
                                          :name (n6 / name
                                                :op1 "England")))
                              :destination (p6 / province
                                    :name (n7 / name
                                          :op1 "Marseille")))
                        :op2 (a8 / attack-01
                              :ARG0 c3
                              :ARG1 p6
                              :time (d3 / date-entity
                                    :year 1904
                                    :season f)))
                  :ARG3 c2))
      :ARG2 c3
      :op3 (p7 / propose-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (a9 / and
                  :op1 (m2 / move-01
                        :ARG1 (u2 / unit
                              :mod c)
                        :ARG2 p6)
                  :op2 (a10 / attack-01
                        :ARG0 c3
                        :ARG1 p6))
            :ARG3 c3))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (tell-01 :ARG0 FRA :ARG1 PRP (AND (attack-01 :ARG0 FRA :ARG1 BEL) ((unit :mod FRA) MTO BUR) (attack-01 :ARG0 AND FRA GER :ARG1 BEL :time (date-entity :year "1904" :season (spring)))) :op2 PRP (AND ((army :mod ENG) RTO MAR) (attack-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 MAR :time (date-entity :year "1904" :season (fall)))))
